***champignon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:champignon.html>champignon</a> (49806)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:champignon.html>champignon</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:champignon.html>champignon</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:champignons.html>champignons</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:champignon.html>champignonnetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:champignon.html>champignon</a></span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:button.html>button</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mushroom.html>mushroom</a>, <i>Agaricus bisporus</i>.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:voeding.html>voeding</a>)</span>, <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:schimmels.html>schimmels</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eetbaar.html>eetbare</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:speciaal.html>speciaal</a> gekweekte <a href = vnd.unilang:witte.html>witte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:paddenstoel.html>paddenstoel</a>; <a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Agaricus_bisporus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Agaricus bisporus"><span style="color:green;"><i>Agaricus bisporus</i></span></a> <img alt="op Wikispecies" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/14px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png" decoding="async" width="14" height="18" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/21px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/28px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 2x" data-file-width="125" data-file-height="160" /> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Agaricus_bitorquis" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Agaricus bitorquis"><span style="color:green;"><i>Agaricus bitorquis</i></span></a> <img alt="op Wikispecies" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/14px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png" decoding="async" width="14" height="18" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/21px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/28px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 2x" data-file-width="125" data-file-height="160" /></li></ol>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:chaser.html>chaser</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">chacer</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">chasour</i>, borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">chaceür</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">chaceor</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">chacier</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:chase.html>chase</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hunt.html>hunt</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> senses <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> influenced <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chase.html>chase</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:pursue.html>pursue</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>. ***cheeseburger.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cheeseburger.html>cheeseburger</a> (11889)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:blend.html>Blend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cheese.html>cheese</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hamburger.html>hamburger</a></i> (1928) 
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Cheeseburger.jpg/220px-Cheeseburger.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Cheeseburger.jpg/330px-Cheeseburger.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Cheeseburger.jpg/440px-Cheeseburger.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="1800" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:cheeseburger.html>cheeseburger</a>.</div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cheeseburger.html>cheeseburger</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cheeseburgers.html>cheeseburgers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hamburger.html>hamburger</a> containing <a href = vnd.unilang:cheese.html>cheese</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:usually.html>usually</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:one.html>one</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:more.html>more</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slices.html>slices</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> processed <a href = vnd.unilang:cheese.html>cheese</a>).
